Dumb boy, as He was named born of KhalvƒÅ·π≠avƒ´ra, the gem in the family of ga·πáakas, got the ability to speak eloquently through the greatness of (the grace of) the Universal Preceptor, invested with sacred thread, and initiated into the entire scripture by his father and taking up asceticism, He remained in the seat of Universal preceptor. Preceptor ≈öa·πÖkarendra (Arbhaka≈õa·πÖkara), after installing MƒÅt·πõgupta, the ardent follower of theprecepts of var·πáƒÅ≈õrama (enjoined for respective classes of people) attained Siddhi on the full moon day in the month of ≈örava·πáa of the ≈öaka year 359. (In the sanskrit and tamil explanations on Pages 22 & 23, Matrugupta appears to be a patron of Sankarendra along with Ramilla, Sri Harsha etc.).
